This program provides a parallel adaptation of a force directed
graph layout algorithm for use with large datasets.
Usage: layout [options] root_file
root_file -- the root name of the file being processed.
root_file.int -- the input file containing the graph to draw using layout.
  The .int file must have the suffix ".int" and each line of .int file
	node_id <tab> node_id <tab> weight
  where node_id's are integers in sequence starting from 0, and
root_file.icoord -- the resulting output file, containing an ordination
  of the graph.  The .icoord file will have the suffix ".icoord" and
  each line of the .icoord file will be of the form
	node_id <tab> x-coord <tab> y-coord
	-s {int>=0} random seed (default value is 0)
	-c {real[0,1]} edge cutting (default 32/40 = .8)
	   (old max was 39/40 = .975)
	-p input parameters from .parms file
	-r {real[0,1]} input coordinates from .real file
	   (hold fixed until fraction of optimization schedule reached)
	-i {int>=0} intermediate output interval (default 0: no output)
	-e output .iedges file (same prefix as .coord file)
